  <script type="text/javascript">
   // before OAS
var BlogoUtils = function(){
    return {
        extractParamFromUri : function(uri, paramName)  {
            if (!uri) {
              return;
            }
            var uri = uri.split('#')[0];  // Remove anchor.
            var parts = uri.split('?');  // Check for query params.
            if (parts.length == 1) {
              return;
            }
            var query = decodeURI(parts[1]);

            // Find url param.
            paramName += '=';
            var params = query.split('&amp;');
            for (var i = 0, param; param = params[i]; ++i) {
              if (param.indexOf(paramName) === 0) {
                return unescape(param.split('=')[1]);
              }
            }
        },

        extractAllParamsFromUri: function(uri) {
            if (!uri) { 
                return; 
            }
            var uri = uri.split('#')[0];  // Remove anchor.
            var parts = uri.split('?');  // Check for query params.
            if (parts.length == 1) { 
                return; 
            }
            return parts[1];
        },
        
        parseInt: function(c) {
            return parseInt(c) || 0;
        },

        cookie : function(name, value, options) {
            if (typeof value != 'undefined') { // name and value given, set cookie
                options = options || {};
                if (value === null) {
                    value = '';
                    options.expires = -1;
                }
                var expires = '';
                if (options.expires &amp;&amp; (typeof options.expires == 'number' || options.expires.toUTCString)) {
                    var date;
                    if (typeof options.expires == 'number') {
                        date = new Date();
                        date.setTime(date.getTime() + (options.expires * 1000));
                    } else {
                        date = options.expires;
                    }
                    expires = '; expires=' + date.toUTCString(); // use expires attribute, max-age is not supported by IE
                }
                var path = options.path ? '; path=' + (options.path) : '';
                var domain = options.domain ? '; domain=' + (options.domain) : '';
                var secure = options.secure ? '; secure' : '';
                document.cookie = [name, '=', encodeURIComponent(value), expires, path, domain, secure].join('');
            } else { // only name given, get cookie
                var cookieValue = null;
                if (document.cookie &amp;&amp; document.cookie != '') {
                    var cookies = document.cookie.split(';');
                    for (var i = 0; i &lt; cookies.length; i++) {
                        var cookie = cookies[i].replace(/^\s+/,'').replace(/\s+$/,'');
                        // Does this cookie string begin with the name we want?
                        if (cookie.substring(0, name.length + 1) == (name + '=')) {
                            cookieValue = decodeURIComponent(cookie.substring(name.length + 1));
                            break;
                        }
                    }
                }
                return cookieValue;
            }
        },

        getSearchKeywords : function(ref) {
            var query_params = [];
            var a = document.createElement('a');
            a.href = ref;
            var urlParts = a.search.split("?");
            var kw = '';
            
            var newQueryString = "";
            if (urlParts.length &gt; 1)
            {
                var parameters = urlParts[1].split("&amp;");
                for (var i=0; (i &lt; parameters.length); i++)
                {
                    var parameterParts = parameters[i].split("=");
                    if (parameterParts[0] == 'q') {
                        kw = parameterParts[1];
                        break;
                    }
                    else if (parameterParts[0] == 'p') {
                        kw = parameterParts[1];
                        break;
                    }
                    else if (parameterParts[0] == 'prev') {
                        kw = blogoUtils.getSearchKeywords(parameterParts[1]);
                        break;
                    }
                }
            }

            return kw;
        },

        checkFirstRefer : function() {
            var lp_firstrefer = blogoUtils.cookie('lp_firstrefer');
            if (lp_firstrefer == null) {
                if (document.referrer) {
                    var search_engines = '.google.,.bing.,.yahoo.,virgilio.,.ask.,.facebook.';
                    var ref = document.referrer;
                    var s_engines = search_engines.split(",");
                    var from_search = false;

                    var keywords = '';

                    if (s_engines.length &gt; 0) {
                        for(var i= 0; i &lt; s_engines.length; i++) {
                            var se = s_engines[i];
                            if (ref.indexOf(se) != -1) {
                                from_search = true;
                                keywords = blogoUtils.getSearchKeywords(ref);
                                break;
                            }
                        }
                    }

                    var name = BlogoConfig.blogName;

                    if (from_search &amp;&amp; keywords.indexOf(name) == -1) {
                        lp_firstrefer = ref;
                    } else
                        lp_firstrefer = 'direct';
                } else {
                    lp_firstrefer = 'direct';
                }
                cookieDomain = document.domain.substring(document.domain.indexOf('.')),
                
                blogoUtils.cookie('lp_firstrefer', lp_firstrefer, { path : '/', domain: cookieDomain, expires : 3600 });
            }
        }
    }
}

var blogoUtils = new BlogoUtils();

blogoUtils.checkFirstRefer();

// Criteo
var crtg_nid = '612';
var crtg_cookiename = 'rta_pops';
var crtg_varname = 'content_pops';

function crtg_getCookie(c_name){ var i,x,y,ARRCookies=document.cookie.split(";");for(i=0;i&lt;ARRCookies.length;i++){x=ARRCookies[i].substr(0,ARRCookies[i].indexOf("="));y=ARRCookies[i].substr(ARRCookies[i].indexOf("=")+1);x=x.replace(/^\s+|\s+$/g,"");if(x==c_name){return unescape(y);} }return'';}

var content_pops = crtg_getCookie(crtg_cookiename);
var crtg_rnd=Math.floor(Math.random()*99999999999);

(function(){
    var crtg_url=location.protocol+'//rtax.criteo.com/delivery/rta/rta.js?netId='+escape(crtg_nid);
    crtg_url +='&amp;cookieName='+escape(crtg_cookiename);
    crtg_url +='&amp;rnd='+crtg_rnd;
    crtg_url +='&amp;varName=' + escape(crtg_varname);
    var crtg_script=document.createElement('script');crtg_script.type='text/javascript';crtg_script.src=crtg_url;crtg_script.async=true;
    if(document.getElementsByTagName("head").length&gt;0)document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(crtg_script);
    else if(document.getElementsByTagName("body").length&gt;0)document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0].appendChild(crtg_script);
})();
  </script>

        var poslist = 'Middle2,x07,TopRight,Right1,x04,Right2,Position2,Top1';

    function track_acq_OAS(OAS_query) {
        if (typeof blogoUtils != 'undefined' &amp;&amp; blogoUtils.cookie) {
            // Take a look at query string
            var OAS_source = (!blogoUtils.cookie('OAS_source')) ? blogoUtils.extractParamFromUri(document.location.href, 'source') : blogoUtils.cookie('OAS_source');
            var OAS_utm_medium = (!blogoUtils.cookie('OAS_utm_medium')) ? blogoUtils.extractParamFromUri(document.location.href, 'utm_medium') : blogoUtils.cookie('OAS_utm_medium');
            var date = new Date();
            // Five minutes...
            date.setTime(date.getTime() + (5 * 60 * 1000));

            if (OAS_source) {
                OAS_query += '&amp;source='+ encodeURIComponent(OAS_source);
                if (!blogoUtils.cookie('OAS_source'))
                    blogoUtils.cookie('OAS_source', OAS_source, { expires : date, path : '/' });
            }
            if (OAS_utm_medium ) {
                OAS_query += '&amp;utm_medium='+ encodeURIComponent(OAS_utm_medium);
                if (!blogoUtils.cookie('OAS_utm_medium'))
                    blogoUtils.cookie('OAS_utm_medium', OAS_utm_medium, { expires : date, path : '/' });
            }
        }
        return OAS_query;
    }

    var call_populis_adserver = {};
    call_populis_adserver.OAS_adstream = 4;
    call_populis_adserver.OAS_listpos = poslist;
    call_populis_adserver.enableDocumentWrite = (poslist != '') ? true : false;

    call_populis_adserver.calladserver = function () {
        var pub = this;
        //var is_mobile = {{options.is_mobile}};
        
        pub.OAS_url = 'http://oas.populisengage.com/';
        var domain_ads = {'it_IT': 'www.blogo.it', 'es_ES': 'es.blogo.it', 'en_US': 'uk.blogo.it', 'fr_FR': 'fr.blogo.it', 'pt_BR': 'www.cidadeinternet.com.br'}
                pub.OAS_sitepage_base   = domain_ads['it_IT'] + '/' + 'cineblog';
        pub.OAS_sitepage_type   = 'article';
        var P_tags              = 'curiosit%C3%A0%2Cposter%2Ctrainspotting%2Cpulp+fiction%2Cavatar%2Cin+evidenza%2C2001+odissea+nello+spazio%2Clocandine+alternative';
        var P_categories        = 'Curiosit%C3%A0%2CPoster%2CFilm+Dc+Comics%2CSuicide+Squad%2CColonne+sonore%2CDichiarazioni%2CLe+Scene+Cult%2CStanley+Kubrick%2CTrailer%2CVideo%2CVintage+Trailer%2CAnticipazioni%2CFilm+2016%2CFoto+dal+set%2CGallery%2CSequel%2CX-Men+%E2%80%93+Giorni+di+un+futuro+passato%2CX-Men%3A+Apocalypse';
        var P_search_js         = 'false';
        var P_geo_country       = 'US';
        var P_geo_region        = 'California';
        var P_geo_district      = 'San Francisco';
        var P_geo_city          = 'San Francisco';
        var P_geo_nielsenarea   = '';
        var OAS_query           = '?kw=' + encodeURIComponent(location.href) ;
        
        OAS_query += '&amp;_RM_HTML_GOOGLEADEX_=yes';
        OAS_query += '&amp;country=' + encodeURIComponent(P_geo_country) + '&amp;region=' + encodeURIComponent(P_geo_region) + '&amp;district=' + encodeURIComponent(P_geo_district);
        OAS_query += '&amp;city=' + encodeURIComponent(P_geo_city) + '&amp;nielsenarea=' + encodeURIComponent(P_geo_nielsenarea);
        OAS_query += '&amp;tags=' + P_tags + '&amp;cat=' + P_categories + '&amp;search_js=' + P_search_js+'&amp;_RM_HTML_SEOTRAFFIC_='+P_search_js+'&amp;seo='+P_search_js;
        OAS_query += '&amp;cookie_enabled=' + navigator.cookieEnabled;
        if (typeof populis_engage_rich_media != 'undefined' &amp;&amp; populis_engage_rich_media == 'yes') {
            OAS_query += '&amp;_RM_HTML_POPULISRICHMEDIA=yes';
        }
                    if (typeof content_pops != 'undefined') { 
                OAS_query += content_pops; 
            }
                
                var OAS_target = '_top';
        //end of configuration
        var OAS_rn = new String (Math.random());
        var OAS_rns = OAS_rn.substring (2, 11);

        OAS_query = track_acq_OAS(OAS_query);

        pub.OAS_query = OAS_query;

        pub.OAS_sitepage_base.replace(/\/$/, '');
        pub.OAS_sitepage_type.replace(/\/$/, '');
        if (pub.OAS_sitepage_base &amp;&amp; pub.OAS_sitepage_base.indexOf(' ') &lt; 0 &amp;&amp; pub.OAS_sitepage_type &amp;&amp; pub.OAS_sitepage_type.indexOf(' ') &lt; 0)
        {
            var sdw ='&lt;sc'+'ript type="text/javascript" src="' + pub.OAS_url + pub.OAS_adstream + '/' + pub.OAS_sitepage_base + '/' + pub.OAS_sitepage_type + '/1' + OAS_rns + '@' + pub.OAS_listpos + OAS_query + '"&gt;&lt;/scr' + 'ipt&gt;';
            if (pub.enableDocumentWrite) {

            } else {
                return sdw;

        }
        return '';
    }

    <div class="content col-xs-12 col-md-8" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/BlogPosting">
     <span itemprop="publisher" itemscope="" itemtype="http://schema.org/Organization">
      <meta content="Cineblog.it" itemprop="name"/>

     <article class="box" id="post_content" itemprop="articleBody">
      <meta content="http://www.cineblog.it/post/34099/locandine-di-film-celebri-da-un-universo-parallelo" itemprop="url"/>
      <meta content="http://media.cineblog.it/th/2012/1/p34099-620x350.jpg" itemprop="image"/>
      <h1 class="title" itemprop="name">
       Locandine di film celebri da un universo parallelo
      </h1>
      <!-- Post Info -->
      <div class="post-info">
       <span>
        Di
        <a class="color-channel" href="/author/839/carloprevosti" itemprop="author" rel="author">
         carloprevosti
        </a>
       </span>
       <span>
        <meta content="2012-01-17T13:40:03+01:00" itemprop="datePublished"/>
        <time datetime="2012-01-17T13:40:03+01:00" itemprop="dateModified">
         marted 17 gennaio 2012
        </time>
       </span>
      </div>
      <p class="schema-descritpion" itemprop="description" style="display:none">
       E se alcuni film famosi fossero stati girati 50 anni fa? Ecco le locandine!
      </p>
      <!-- SOCIAL SHARE -->
      <!-- data-attribute = utilizzati in versione desktop -->

      <!-- post content -->
      <p>
       <a href="http://www.cineblog.it/galleria/film-da-un-altro-universo/">
        <img alt="Film da un altro universo" class="post" height="462" src="http://media.cineblog.it/f/fil/film-da-un-altro-universo/01.jpg" width="586"/>
       </a>
       <br clear="all"/>
      </p>
      <p>
       Come sarebbero stati alcuni tra i pi celebri film degli ultimi dieci anni se questi fossero stati realizzati almeno mezzo secolo fa, magari in un universo parallelo?
      </p>
      <p>
       A questa strampalata domanda hanno cercato di dare una risposta sul blog
       <a href="http://www.behance.net">
        Behance
       </a>
       , dove si sono divertiti a ipotizzare delle locandine ad hoc per ogni film, scegliendo anche degli attori "alternativi" che avrebbero preso il posto di protagonista di ciascuna pellicola...
      </p>
      <p>
       Ammetto che alcune idee potrebbero solleticare la fantasia di tanti cinefili, come un
       <a href="http://www.cineblog.it/tag/2001 Odissea nello spazio">
        2001 Odissea nello spazio
       </a>
       in versione
       <a href="http://www.cineblog.it/tag/fritz lang">
        Fritz Lang
       </a>
       tanto per citarne uno...
      </p>
      <p>

        <textarea name="comment_text">
        </textarea>
        <div class="thumb">
         <!-- image( 30x30 )-->
         <img alt="" class="lazy avatar_image" data-original="#" height="30" src="" style="display: block;" width="30"/>

       </i>

       Vedi pi commenti
       <i class="blogoicon-loader">

     <script type="text/javascript">
      (function($, BlogoConfig, BlogoUser, CommentBox){

		var currentUrl    = window.location.href;

		var $fbButton     = $("#fbLoginButton");
		var $container    = $("#comments-container");
		var $reload       = $("#reload");
		var $loadMore     = $("#load-more");
		var $commentForm  = $("form#commentform");
		var $orderSelect  = $("#selected-order");
		var $orderLinks   = $("#change-order&gt;li&gt;a");
		var $mobileOrder     = $("#mobile-order");
		var $commentCount = $("#comment-count");

		CommentBox = $.extend(CommentBox,{

			options: {
				postId: 34099,
				limit: 5,
				loginUrl: BlogoConfig.communityUrl+"/entra?returnUrl="+currentUrl+"#comments"
			},
		
			setCookie: function(cname, cvalue, exdays) {
			    var d = new Date();
			    var exdays = typeof exdays !== 'undefined' ? exdays : 30;
			    d.setTime(d.getTime() + (exdays*24*60*60*1000));
			    var expires = "expires="+d.toUTCString();
			    document.cookie = cname + "=" + cvalue + "; " + expires;
			},
			getCookie: function(cname) {
			    var name = cname + "=";
			    var ca = document.cookie.split(';');
			    for(var i=0; i&lt;ca.length; i++) {
			        var c = ca[i];
			        while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1);
			        if (c.indexOf(name) == 0) return c.substring(name.length, c.length);
			    }
			    return "";
			},
			checkCookie: function(cname) {
			    var cookie = CommentBox.getCookie(cname);
			    if (cookie != "") {
			        return true;
			    }
			    return false;
			},
        	getTotal: function() {
        		return parseInt($commentCount.text());
        	},
		    addComment: function(data, order, newCommentCount, isNew)
		    {
		    	console.log(data);
		        var newCommentCount = typeof newCommentCount !== 'undefined' ? newCommentCount : false;
		        var display_date = typeof data.display_date !== 'undefined' ? data.display_date : data.publish_date;
		        var notifyText = "Notifica abuso";
		        var commentNumber = 0;
		        if(!newCommentCount) {
		            var currentSelectedOrder = $('#selected-order').data('order');
		            if(currentSelectedOrder == 'desc') {
		                commentNumber = parseInt($( "#comment-list&gt;li" ).last().data("count"))-1;
		            } else {
		                commentNumber = parseInt($( "#comment-list&gt;li" ).last().data("count"))+1;
		            }
		        } else {
		            commentNumber = newCommentCount;
		        }

		        var avatar = (data.avatar !== null &amp;&amp; data.avatar !== undefined) ? data.avatar : 'http://static-bn.blogo.it/bn/img/user_img_placeholder.png';
		    
		        
		        if(data.id_community != '') {
		        	var userUrl = ' href="'+BlogoConfig.communityUrl+'/profilo/condivisioni/'+data.username+'" ';
		        	var thumbTag = "&lt;a target='_blank'" + userUrl + "title='Guarda le ultime attivit di " + data.nickname + "' class='thumb'&gt;&lt;img width='50' height='50' alt='" + data.nickname + "' data-original='" + avatar + "' class='lazy' src='" + avatar + "' style='display: block;'&gt;&lt;/a&gt;";
		            var urlTag = "&lt;a target='_blank'" + userUrl + "class='user color-channel h-secondary-color-channel'&gt;" + data.nickname + "&lt;/a&gt;";
		        } else {
		        	var thumbTag = "&lt;span class='thumb'&gt;&lt;img width='50' height='50' alt='" + data.nickname + "' data-original='" + avatar + "' class='lazy' src='" + avatar + "' style='display: block;'&gt;&lt;/span&gt;";
		            var urlTag = "&lt;span class='user color-channel h-secondary-color-channel'&gt;" + data.nickname + "&lt;/span&gt;";		        	
		        }

		        var markup;
		        if(!isNew){
			        markup = 
			            "&lt;li class='item-comment' id='comment-" + data.id_comment + "' data-count='"+commentNumber+"'&gt; \
			                " + thumbTag + " \
			                &lt;div class='data'&gt; \
			                    &lt;div class='head'&gt; \
			                        " + urlTag + " \
			                        &lt;span class='meta'&gt; \
			                            &lt;a title='" + data.publish_date + "' href='#comment-" + data.id_comment + "' class='h-color-channel'&gt;#"+commentNumber+"&lt;/a&gt; \
			                            &lt;time datetime='" + data.publish_date + "'&gt;" + display_date + "&lt;/time&gt; \
			                        &lt;/span&gt; \
			                    &lt;/div&gt; \
			                    &lt;div class='text' id='commenttext-" + data.id_comment + "'&gt;&lt;/div&gt; \
			                    &lt;div class='moderation'&gt; \
			                        &lt;a href='#' data-comment='" + data.id_comment + "'&gt;&lt;span&gt;"+notifyText+"&lt;/span&gt; &lt;i class='blogoicon-abuse'&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/a&gt; \
			                    &lt;/div&gt; \
			                &lt;/div&gt; \
			            &lt;/li&gt;";

			        if(order == 'asc') {
			            $( "#comment-list" ).append(markup);

			        } else {
			            $( "#comment-list" ).prepend(markup);
			        }
		    	}else{
		    		markup = thumbTag + " \
			                &lt;div class='data'&gt; \
			                    &lt;div class='head'&gt; \
			                        " + urlTag + " \
			                        &lt;span class='meta'&gt; \
			                            &lt;a title='" + data.publish_date + "' href='#comment-" + data.id_comment + "' class='h-color-channel'&gt;#"+commentNumber+"&lt;/a&gt; \
			                            &lt;time datetime='" + data.publish_date + "'&gt;" + display_date + "&lt;/time&gt; \
			                        &lt;/span&gt; \
			                    &lt;/div&gt; \
			                    &lt;div class='text' id='commenttext-" + data.id_comment + "'&gt;&lt;/div&gt; \
			                    &lt;div class='moderation'&gt; \
			                        &lt;a href='#' data-comment='" + data.id_comment + "'&gt;&lt;span&gt;"+notifyText+"&lt;/span&gt; &lt;i class='blogoicon-abuse'&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/a&gt; \
			                    &lt;/div&gt; \
			                &lt;/div&gt;";


			        //add attributes to new comment
		            $(commentLoading).attr('id', 'comment-' + data.id_comment  );
					$(commentLoading).attr('data-count', commentNumber );
		            $(commentLoading).append(markup);

		            //effects
		            setTimeout(function(){ $(commentLoading).css('height', commentLoading.scrollHeight); },0) 
					setTimeout(function(){ $(commentLoading).addClass('loaded-comment'); },500);
					setTimeout(function(){ $(commentLoading).removeClass('loading-comment'); },1000);


		    	}

		        // insert comment text as html //console.log(data.comment);
		        $("div#commenttext-"+data.id_comment).html(data.comment);
		    },
		    renderUserInfo: function() {

		    	if(!BlogoUser.loggedInCommunity &amp;&amp; !BlogoUser.loggedInFacebook) {
		    		return;
		    	}

		    	$('#notLoggedForm').hide();
		    	$('#loggedForm').css('display', 'inline-block');
		    	

		    	if (BlogoConfig.pageType == 'post' &amp;&amp; BlogoUser.userdata.avatar &amp;&amp; BlogoUser.userdata.visibleName) {
		            $('img.avatar_image').attr('src', BlogoUser.userdata.avatar).show();
		            $('span.username').html(BlogoUser.userdata.visibleName).show();
		        } else {
		        	$('img.avatar_image').hide();
		            $('span.username').hide();
		        }

		        $('input#submit-cmt').prop('disabled', true);

		    },
			loadComments: function(order) {

		        var id = CommentBox.options.postId;
		        var page = typeof page !== 'undefined' ? page : 1;
		        var limit = CommentBox.options.limit;
		        var params = { 
		        	page : page 
		        };

		        $.get( "/ajax/get-comments/"+id+"/"+order, params, function( data ) {
		            $container.html(data);
		            	                
		            $loadMore.data("page", page);
		            if(CommentBox.getTotal() &gt; limit) {
		                $loadMore.show();
		            }

		            //Remove loader
		            $container.addClass('loaded-comment');
		            setTimeout(function(){ $container.removeClass('loading-comment'); },500);

		        });
	       	},
	       	loadMore: function(order, page) {
			   	
			   	var id = CommentBox.options.postId;
			    var page  = typeof page !== 'undefined' ? page : 1;
			    var params = { 
			    	page : page, 
			    	limit : 20
			    };

			    //add loader
			    $loadMore.addClass('loading-comments')
			    
			    $.getJSON( "/ajax/get-comments/"+id+"/"+order+'/json', params , function( data ) {
			        $.each( data.results, function( key, val ) {
			            CommentBox.addComment(val, 'asc');
			        });
			        var totalLi = $( "#comment-list&gt;li" ).length;
			        if( totalLi &lt; data.total ) {
			            $loadMore.data("page", page);
			        } else {
			            $loadMore.hide();
			        }

			        //remove loader
			        $loadMore.removeClass('loading-comments');
			    });
	       	},

        	events: {

        		onFbButtonClick: function (event) 
        		{
        			event.preventDefault();
        			fbManager.fbLogin();
            		return false;
        		},
        		onOrderChange: function(event)
        		{
        			event.preventDefault();
		            var order = $(this).data('value');
		            var text = $(this).text();

		            //Add loader
		            $container.removeClass('loaded-comment').addClass('loading-comment');

		            $orderSelect.data('order', order).html(text);
		            $('div.sort').removeClass('open');
		            CommentBox.loadComments(order);
        		},
        	    onOrderMobileChange: function(event)
        		{
        			event.preventDefault();
        			var order = '';
		            if($(this).data('order') == 'asc') {
		            	order = 'desc';
		            } else {
		            	order = 'asc';
		            }
		            //Add loader
		            $container.removeClass('loaded-comment').addClass('loading-comment');
		            $mobileOrder.data('order', order);
		            CommentBox.loadComments(order);
        		},	
			  	onLoadMoreClick: function (event)
			    {
			    	event.preventDefault();
		            var order = $orderSelect.data('order');
		            var page = parseInt($loadMore.data('page'))+1;
			    	CommentBox.loadMore(order, page);
			    },
			  	onReloadClick: function (event)
			    {
			    	event.preventDefault();
		            var order = $orderSelect.data('order');
            		CommentBox.loadComments(order);
			    },
			    onFormSubmit: function (event)
			    {
			    	event.preventDefault();

			    	$('input#submit-cmt').prop('disabled', true);

		            // check current user
		         	if(!BlogoUser.loggedInCommunity &amp;&amp; !BlogoUser.loggedInFacebook) {
		         	    window.location.href= CommentBox.options.loginUrl;
		         	    return;
		         	}
		            
		            var commentCount = CommentBox.getTotal()+1;
		            var order = $orderSelect.data('order');



		            //add loader
		            $(".loading-comment").remove();
					commentLoading = document.createElement("li");
					commentLoading.style.display = 'none';
					commentLoading.className = 'item-comment loading-comment';
					commentLoading.innerHTML = '&lt;i class="blogoicon-loader"&gt;&lt;/i&gt;';
					$('#comment-list').prepend(commentLoading);
					$(commentLoading).fadeIn(500);



		            $.post( "/ajax/submit-comment", $(this).serialize() )
		                .done(function( data ) {
		                    if(data.success) {          
		                        CommentBox.addComment(data.data, 'desc', commentCount, 1);
		                        $commentCount.html(commentCount);
		                    } else {
		                    	$(".user-logged .error").remove();
		                    	$("#submit-cmt").after("&lt;p class=\"error\"&gt;" + data.message + "&lt;/p&gt;");
		                    	$(".loading-comment").remove();
		                    } 
		                    $commentForm[0].reset();
		                    $('input#submit-cmt').prop('disabled', true);

		                    CommentBox.events.handleTextArea();
		                });

					
			    },
			  	onAbuseClick: function (event)
			    {
			    	event.preventDefault();
			    	var id = $(this).data('comment');
			    	var abuseCookie = CommentBox.checkCookie('abuseSent_'+id);
			    	var notifySentText = "Notifica di abuso inviata.";
			    	if(id != false &amp;&amp; !abuseCookie) {
				    	console.log("/ajax/abuse-comment/"+id);
				    	$.get( "/ajax/abuse-comment/"+id)
					    	.done(function( data ) {
					    		if(data.success) {
					    			CommentBox.setCookie('abuseSent_'+id, 1);
			                    	$(this).data('comment', false);
			                    }
			                });
				    }
				    $(this).html('&lt;span style="opacity:1"&gt;'+notifySentText+'&lt;/span&gt;');
			    },
			    handleTextArea: function(){
			    	$(".user-logged textarea").keyup(function() {
			    		console.log("handleTextArea");
						if($(this).val().length == 0)
							$('.user-logged #submit-cmt').attr('disabled', true);
						else
							$('.user-logged #submit-cmt').attr('disabled', false);
					});
			    }
        	}

		});

		// listen to FBManager events so we are sure it's loaded
		$( window ).on('FBManager.init_finish', function() {
			$fbButton.on('click', CommentBox.events.onFbButtonClick);
			$orderLinks.on('click', CommentBox.events.onOrderChange);
			$mobileOrder.on('click', CommentBox.events.onOrderMobileChange);
			$loadMore.on('click', CommentBox.events.onLoadMoreClick);
			$reload.on('click', CommentBox.events.onReloadClick);
			$commentForm.on('submit', CommentBox.events.onFormSubmit);
			$container.on('click', 'div.moderation&gt;a', CommentBox.events.onAbuseClick);
			CommentBox.loadComments('asc'); // load comment fbManager.fbLogin()
			CommentBox.events.handleTextArea();

		});

		$( window ).on('FBManager.init_finish FBManager.facebook_data_loaded', function() {

			CommentBox.renderUserInfo(); // render user info on form
		});

	})(jQuery, BlogoConfig, BlogoUser, (typeof CommentBox === 'undefined' ? {} : CommentBox));
     </script>

     <script>
      function adBlockDetected() {
		    console.log ( 'adBlock_Detected' );
		    if(typeof smartbox == 'undefined'){
		        $.ajax({
		            type: 'POST',
		            url: 'http://p.as-farm.com/lap/68072.html?imgPrefix=http://p.as-farm.com/lap/',
		            data:{
		                cookies: navigator.cookieEnabled,
		                url: window.location.href
		            },
		            success: function(data, textStatus, jqXHR){
		                $('#ligatus_ad_container_populis_tvnews_mobile').after(data); 
		            }
		        });
		    }
		}
		function adBlockNotDetected() {
		    console.log ( 'adBlock_NOT_Detected' );
		}

		if(typeof fuckAdBlock === 'undefined') {
		    adBlockDetected();
		} else {
		    fuckAdBlock.onDetected(adBlockDetected).onNotDetected(adBlockNotDetected);
		}

		function checkAgain() {
		    fuckAdBlock.onDetected(adBlockDetected).onNotDetected(adBlockNotDetected);
		    setTimeout(function() {
		        fuckAdBlock.check();
		    }, 500);
		}
     </script>

  <!-- PLUGIN: Facebook-->
  <div id="fb-root">
  </div>
  <script type="text/javascript">
   // new FbManager
var FBManager = function(FB)
{
    var pub = this;
    var _p  = {};

    // FB object
    _p.FB   = FB;

    // the current FB user status
    _p.currentUserFbStatus = 'unknown';

    // auto-sharing enabled from BlogoUser?
    _p.frictionlessSharingEnabled = BlogoUser.shareAppActive;

    // timeout for auto-sharing
    _p.frictionlessSharingTimeout = 10000;

    // articles read on fb
    _p.articles             = null;
    _p.articlesPerPages     = 4;
    _p.articlesCurrentPage  = 0;
    _p.fb_pushing           = false;

    // check if a console exists
    if (typeof console == "undefined")
        _p.console = { log: function() {} };
    else
        _p.console = console;

    var debugging = false;

    if (!debugging)
        _p.console = { log: function() {} };
    
    _p.isPushing = function() {
        return _p.fb_pushing;
    };
    _p.setPushing = function( _v ) {
        _p.fb_pushing = _v;
    };
    _p.getPermalink = function () {
        var permalink = (_p.permalink) ? _p.permalink : window.location.href;
        var _url = permalink.replace(/#.*/, "");
        return _url;
    }

    // init 
    pub.init = function() {
        
        _p.console.log('FBManager init');
        
        // check Fb login status
        _p.FB.getLoginStatus(function(response) {
            
            if (response.status === 'connected') {

                _p.console.log('Connected to FB');
                _p.currentUserFbStatus = 'connected';

                var accessToken = response.authResponse.accessToken;

                // if the user is logged to community there is no need to continue
                if (BlogoUser.loggedInCommunity) {
                    _p.console.log('Connected to "Community"');
                    _p.handleTabArticles();
                    return;
                } 

                if (! BlogoUser.loggedInFacebook) {
                    // checks if the user is registered to community and inits the interface
                    $.ajax({
                        url: BlogoConfig.siteUrl + '/ajax/is-logged',
                        xhrFields: {withCredentials: true},
                        dataType: 'json',
                        data: { 'accessToken': accessToken },
                        success: function(data, status, xhr) {
                            _p.initInterface(data, response, xhr);
                        },
                    });
                }
            } else {
                _p.console.log('Not connected to FB, the current user status is: "' + response.status + '"');
            }
        });

        // triggers an event for data loaded
        $(window).trigger('FBManager.init_finish');
    };

    pub.fbLogin = function(){
        if (_p.FB) {
            _p.FB.login(function(response) {
                if (response.status == 'connected') {
    
                    _p.console.log('Connected to FB');
                    _p.currentUserFbStatus = 'connected';
                    
                    var accessToken = response.authResponse.accessToken;

                    // checks if the user is registered to community and inits the interface
                    $.ajax({
                        url: BlogoConfig.siteUrl + '/ajax/is-logged',
                        xhrFields: {withCredentials: true},
                        dataType: 'json',
                        data: { 'accessToken': accessToken, 'onlyFbLogin': true },
                        success: function(data, status, xhr) {
                            _p.initInterface(data, response, xhr);
                        },
                    });
                }
             }, { scope: 'email' });
        } else {
            _p.console.log('FB Object not present');
        }


    };

    // renders the html for the menu and the comment box
    _p.initInterface = function(data, response, xhr) {
        if (data.ret == 'ok' &amp;&amp; data.userdata) {
            // sets the current FB user status
            _p.currentUserFbStatus = 'connected';

            // sets the BlogoUser object
            BlogoUser.loggedInCommunity     = data.logged;
            BlogoUser.loggedInFacebook      = true;
            BlogoUser.userdata.avatar       = data.userdata.avatar;
            BlogoUser.userdata.visibleName  = data.userdata.visibleName;

            // triggers an event for data loaded
            $(window).trigger('FBManager.facebook_data_loaded');

            // is logged to community
            if (data.logged) {
                // replaces the menu
                if (data.profile_menu) {
                    _p.console.log('Rendering Menu');
                    $('#nav-profile').replaceWith(data.profile_menu);
                    $('#fbAct_Logout').bind('click', {}, _p.logout );
                }
                // sets shareAppActive
                if (data.userdata.shareAppActive) {
                    _p.frictionlessSharingEnabled = data.userdata.shareAppActive;
                }
            }
            // renders the shared articles
            _p.handleTabArticles();
        } else {
            _p.console.log(data.message);
        }
    };

    pub.postAction = function() {
        if (_p.isPushing()) {
            _p.console.log('Pushing news.reads in progress...');
            return;
        }
        if (_p.isCurrentArticleAlreadyPushed()) {
            _p.console.log('Current article is already pushed...');
            return;
        }
        _p.setPushing(true);
        _p.fbPostAction(_p.fbPostedAction);
    };

    _p.fbPostAction = function(_callback) {
        var permalink = _p.getPermalink();
        _p.FB.api(
            '/me/news.reads?article=' + encodeURIComponent( permalink ),
            'post',
            function(response) {
                if (!response || response.error) {
                    if (response.error) {
                       _p.console.log(response.error.message); 
                    }
                } else {
                    _p.current_url_id = response.id;
                    if (typeof _callback != 'undefined')
                        _callback(response);
                    _p.console.log(response.id); 
                }
        });
    }

    _p.fbPostedAction = function(_response) {
        _p.FB.api(
            '/'+_response.id,
            'get',
            function(response) {
               if (!response || response.error) {
                   _p.console.log(response.error.message);
               } else {
                   _p.console.log('Fb news.reads pushed');
                   _p.console.log(response);
                   _p.articles.splice(0,0,response);
                   _p.renderTabArticles();
               }
        });
    };

    _p.isCurrentArticleAlreadyPushed = function () {
        if (!_p.articles)
            return false;
        var _data = _p.articles;
        var _url = _p.getPermalink();
        var article_url = null;
        for(var n in _data ) {
            article_url = _data[n].data.article.url;
            if (article_url == _url) {
                // Disable 
                return true;
            }
        }
        return false;
    };

    _p.handleTabArticles = function() {
        _p.FB.api('/me/permissions', function(response) {
            if (response.error)  {
                _p.console.log('/me error: ' + response.error );
                return;
            }

            var publish_permission = false;
            if (response.data &amp;&amp; response.data.length &gt; 0) { 
                for (i in response.data) {
                    if (response.data[i].permission == 'publish_actions' &amp;&amp; response.data[i].status == 'granted') {
                        publish_permission = true;
                    }
                }
            }
            
            if (publish_permission) {
                _p.console.log('FB publish permission granted');
                _p.fbGetActivitiesHistory(_p.gotActivitiesHistory);
                if (_p.frictionlessSharingEnabled &amp;&amp; BlogoConfig.pageType == 'post') {
                    window.setTimeout(pub.postAction, _p.frictionlessSharingTimeout);
                }
            } else {
                _p.console.log('No FB publish permission');
                _p.frictionlessSharingEnabled = false
            }
        });
    };

    _p.gotActivitiesHistory = function() {
        _p.renderTabArticles();
    };

    _p.fbGetActivitiesHistory = function (_targetFunct, _offset, _limit) {
        if (typeof _offset == 'undefined') 
            _offset = '0';
        if (typeof _limit == 'undefined') 
            _limit = '100';
        _p.FB.api (
            '/me/news.reads',
            { method: 'get', limit: _limit, offset: _offset},
            function(response) {
               if (!response || response.error) {
                   _p.console.log(response.error.message); 
               } else {
                    if ( response.data ) {
                        _p.articles = response.data;
                        _targetFunct();
                    } 
                    else {
                        _p.console.log('No FB news.reads data found');
                    }
               }
        });
    };

    // renders the article's box
    _p.renderTabArticles = function () {

        var _data = _p.articles;
        if (_data == null)
            return;
        var totalPages = Math.ceil(_data.length/_p.articlesPerPages);
        var itemsCounter = 0;
        if (_p.articlesCurrentPage &lt; 0)
            _p.articlesCurrentPage = 0;
        if (_p.articlesCurrentPage &gt;= totalPages)
            _p.articlesCurrentPage = totalPages-1;

        $('#fbAct_Pages').text((_p.articlesCurrentPage+1)+"/"+totalPages);

        if (_data.length) {
            var start = _p.articlesCurrentPage*_p.articlesPerPages;
            var end = Math.min(start+_p.articlesPerPages, _data.length) ;

            // deletes all &lt;li&gt; except title
            $("ul.readarticles li:gt(0)").remove();

            for (var n = start; n &lt; end; n++) {
                var title = (_data[n].data.article.title.length &gt;  _p.maxTitleLength ) ? _data[n].data.article.title.slice(0, _p.maxTitleLength - 1)+"..." : _data[n].data.article.title;
                var tpl ='';
                tpl += '&lt;li class="small"&gt;&lt;a href="'+_data[n].data.article.url+'" id="fbAct_ArticleAnchor_' + _data[n].id + '"&gt;&lt;span&gt;'+title+'&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/a&gt;&lt;span class="deleteRead" id="fbAct_ArticleDelete_' + _data[n].id + '"&gt;&lt;i class="blogoicon-plus"&gt;&lt;/i&gt;&lt;/span&gt;&lt;/li&gt;';
                $('.readarticles').append(tpl);
                $('#fbAct_ArticleDelete_'+_data[n].id).bind('click',
                     { id : _data[n].id, callback: _p.removeArticlesPaged },
                     _p.clickDeleteAction );
                itemsCounter++;
            }
        }
        $('.sharedarticles').show();
                
        totalPages &gt; 1 
            ? $('#fbAct_PageTab').show() 
            : $('#fbAct_PageTab').hide();
        
        $('#fbAct_PagesPrev').click(-1, _p.clickShowArticlesPaged);
        $('#fbAct_PagesNext').click( 1, _p.clickShowArticlesPaged);
    };

    _p.deleteArticle = function(_id) {
       for (c in _p.articles) {
           if (_p.articles[c].id == _id) {
               _p.articles.splice(c,1);
               _p.renderTabArticles();
               break;
           }
       }
    };

    _p.clickDeleteAction = function(_e) {
        _e.stopPropagation();
        if (typeof _e != 'undefined' &amp;&amp; _e.data.id &amp;&amp; _e.data.callback) {
            var anchor_id = '#fbAct_ArticleAnchor_'+_e.data.id;
            var span_id = '#fbAct_ArticleDelete_'+_e.data.id;
            $(anchor_id).css({ opacity: 0.5 });
            $(span_id).removeClass('deleteRead').addClass('deleteLoad')
            _p.fbDeleteAction(_e.data.id, _e.data.callback);
        }
        return false;
    };

    _p.removeArticlesPaged = function (_response) {
        _p.renderTabArticles();
    };

    _p.fbDeleteAction = function(_id, _callback){
        _p.FB.api(
            '/'+ _id,
            'delete',
            function(response) {
               if (!response || response.error) {
                    // Ugly hack... delete in any case.
                   _p.deleteArticle(_id);
                   if (_callback)
                       _callback(response);
                   _p.console.log(response.error.message); 
               } else {
                   _p.deleteArticle(_id);
                   if (_callback)
                       _callback(response);
                   _p.console.log('Fb news.reads delete done successfully'); 
                   _p.renderTabArticles();
               }
        });
    };

    _p.clickShowArticlesPaged = function (_e) {
        if (typeof _e != "undefined") {
            _e.preventDefault();
            _p.articlesCurrentPage += _e.data;
        }
        _p.renderTabArticles();
    };

    _p.logout = function(e) {        
        e.preventDefault();
        var href = this.href;

        if (_p.currentUserFbStatus == 'connected') {
            _p.FB.logout(function(response) {
                // if is a community member redirects to the project 
                if (BlogoUser.loggedInCommunity) {
                    window.location.href=href;
                }
            });
        }
        window.location.href=href;
    }

    $('#fbAct_Logout').bind('click', {}, _p.logout );

    return pub;
}

window.fbAsyncInit = function() {
    FB.init({
        appId      : BlogoConfig.fbAppId,
        version    : 'v2.2',
        xfbml      : 1,
        cookie     : true
    });
    window.fbManager = new FBManager(FB);
    window.fbManager.init();
};

    fjs.parentNode.insertBefore(js, fjs);
}(document, 'script', 'facebook-jssdk'));

   window.twttr = (function(d, s, id) {
  var js, fjs = d.getElementsByTagName(s)[0],
    t = window.twttr || {};
  if (d.getElementById(id)) return;
  js = d.createElement(s);
  js.id = id;
  js.src = "https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js";
  fjs.parentNode.insertBefore(js, fjs);
 
  t._e = [];
  t.ready = function(f) {
    t._e.push(f);
  };
 
  return t;
}(document, "script", "twitter-wjs"));

  <script type="text/javascript">
   //&lt;!--
    var RatingManager = function(_window, $, BlogoUser, BlogoConfig)
{
    var pub = this;

    var _p = {};
    _p.window         = _window;
    _p.ratingHasVoted = false;
    _p.ratingCount    = 0;
    _p.ratingValue    = 0;
    _p.bestRating     = 5.00;
    _p.postId         = 0;
    _p.messages       = {};
    _p.url            = '';
    _p.communityUrl   = '';

    _p.renderRateBox = function() {
        if ($.fn.raty) {
            $('#stars-rating').raty({
                path: 'http://static-q.blogo.it/s/sf/img/raty',
                score: _p.ratingValue,
                click: function(score, evt) {
                    // alert('ID: ' + $(this).attr('id') + "\nscore: " + score + "\nevent: " + evt);
                    if (_p.ratingHasVoted)

                        $('#stars-message').html(_p.messages.messageAlreadyVoted);
                    else {
                        $('#stars-message').html(_p.messages.messageVoting);
                        var callback = function(data) {
                            data = data || {};
                            if (data.status) {
                                _p.ratingHasVoted = true;
                                var newRatingCount = (_p.ratingCount + 1);
                                var newRatingValue = ((_p.ratingValue * _p.ratingCount) + score) / newRatingCount;
                                var template = "&lt;span &gt;" + parseFloat(newRatingValue).toFixed(2) + "&lt;/span&gt; " + _p.messages.messageLabelOn + " " + parseFloat(_p.bestRating).toFixed(2) + " " + _p.messages.messageLabelBased + ' ' + _p.messages.messageLabelOn + " &lt;strong&gt;"+ newRatingCount + "&lt;/strong&gt; " + (newRatingCount == 1 ? _p.messages.messageLabelVote : _p.messages.messageLabelVotes) + ".&lt;/span&gt;";
                                $('#stars-description').html(template);
                                $('#stars-message').html(_p.messages.messageRegistered);
                            } else {
                                if (data.message &amp;&amp; data.message == 'already_voted') {
                                    _p.ratingHasVoted = true;
                                    $('#stars-message').html(_p.messages.messageAlreadyVoted);
                                } else
                                    $('#stars-message').html(_p.messages.messageError);
                            }
                        };
                        _p.ratePost(score, callback);
                    }
                }
            });
        }
    };

    _p.ratePost = function(score, callback){

        _p.submit_in_process = true;

        if (BlogoUser.loggedInCommunity || BlogoUser.loggedInFacebook || BlogoConfig.cluster == 'blogosfere') {
            // Autenticato
            var data_rate = {
                'url' : _p.url,
                'type' : 'post',
                'data' : {
                    'score': score,
                    'post_id' : _p.postId
                },
                'dataType' : 'json'
            };
            $.ajax(data_rate).done(function(e) {

                if(e.message == 'unlogged') {
                    $('#stars-description').html(_p.messages.messageAuthRequired);
                    $('#stars-message').html('');
                    var timeoutID = window.setTimeout(function() {
                        _p.window.location = _p.communityUrl + encodeURIComponent(_p.getPermalink()+"#goto_stars_rating");
                    }, 4000);
                } else {
                    try {
                        callback(e);
                    } catch (e) {}
                }
                _p.submit_in_process = false;
            });
        } else {
            $('#stars-description').html(_p.messages.messageAuthRequired);
            $('#stars-message').html('');
            var timeoutID = window.setTimeout(function() {
                _p.window.location = _p.communityUrl + encodeURIComponent(_p.getPermalink()+"#goto_stars_rating");
            }, 4000);
        }

       return false;
    };

    _p.getPermalink = function () {
        var permalink = (_p.permalink) ? _p.permalink : window.location.href;
        var _url = permalink.replace(/#.*/, "");

        return _url;
    }

    _p.getSiteAddress = function() {
        return BlogoConfig.siteUrl;
    };

    pub.init = function() {
        _p.renderRateBox();
    };

    pub.setUrl = function(url) {
        _p.url = url;

        return pub;
    }

    pub.setCommunityUrl = function(communityUrl) {
        _p.communityUrl = communityUrl;

        return pub;
    }

    pub.setRatingValue = function(ratingValue) {
        _p.ratingValue = ratingValue;

        return pub;
    }

    pub.setRatingCount = function(ratingCount) {
        _p.ratingCount = ratingCount;

        return pub;
    }

    pub.setMessages = function(messages) {
        _p.messages = messages;

        return pub;
    }

    pub.setPostId = function(postId) {
        _p.postId = postId;

        return pub;
    }

    return pub;

};

/*!
 * jQuery Raty - A Star Rating Plugin
 * ------------------------------------------------------------------
 *
 * jQuery Raty is a plugin that generates a customizable star rating.
 *
 * Licensed under The MIT License
 *
 * @version        2.5.2
 * @since          2010.06.11
 * @author         Washington Botelho
 * @documentation  wbotelhos.com/raty
 *
 * ------------------------------------------------------------------
 *
 *  &lt;div id="star"&gt;&lt;/div&gt;
 *
 *  $('#star').raty();
 *
 */
;(function($) {

  var methods = {
    init: function(settings) {
      return this.each(function() {
        methods.destroy.call(this);

        this.opt = $.extend(true, {}, $.fn.raty.defaults, settings);

        var that  = $(this),
            inits = ['number', 'readOnly', 'score', 'scoreName'];

        methods._callback.call(this, inits);

        if (this.opt.precision) {
          methods._adjustPrecision.call(this);
        }

        this.opt.number = methods._between(this.opt.number, 0, this.opt.numberMax)

        this.opt.path = this.opt.path || '';

        if (this.opt.path &amp;&amp; this.opt.path.slice(this.opt.path.length - 1, this.opt.path.length) !== '/') {
          this.opt.path += '/';
        }

        this.stars = methods._createStars.call(this);
        this.score = methods._createScore.call(this);

        methods._apply.call(this, this.opt.score);

        var space  = this.opt.space ? 4 : 0,
            width  = this.opt.width || (this.opt.number * this.opt.size + this.opt.number * space);

        if (this.opt.cancel) {
          this.cancel = methods._createCancel.call(this);

          width += (this.opt.size + space);
        }

        if (this.opt.readOnly) {
          methods._lock.call(this);
        } else {
          that.css('cursor', 'pointer');
          methods._binds.call(this);
        }

        if (this.opt.width !== false) {
          that.css('width', width);
        }

        methods._target.call(this, this.opt.score);

        that.data({ 'settings': this.opt, 'raty': true });
      });
    }, _adjustPrecision: function() {
      this.opt.targetType = 'score';
      this.opt.half       = true;
    }, _apply: function(score) {
      if (score &amp;&amp; score &gt; 0) {
        score = methods._between(score, 0, this.opt.number);
        this.score.val(score);
      }

      methods._fill.call(this, score);

      if (score) {
        methods._roundStars.call(this, score);
      }
    }, _between: function(value, min, max) {
      return Math.min(Math.max(parseFloat(value), min), max);
    }, _binds: function() {
      if (this.cancel) {
        methods._bindCancel.call(this);
      }

      methods._bindClick.call(this);
      methods._bindOut.call(this);
      methods._bindOver.call(this);
    }, _bindCancel: function() {
      methods._bindClickCancel.call(this);
      methods._bindOutCancel.call(this);
      methods._bindOverCancel.call(this);
    }, _bindClick: function() {
      var self = this,
          that = $(self);

      self.stars.on('click.raty', function(evt) {
        self.score.val((self.opt.half || self.opt.precision) ? that.data('score') : this.alt);

        if (self.opt.click) {
          self.opt.click.call(self, parseFloat(self.score.val()), evt);
        }
      });
    }, _bindClickCancel: function() {
      var self = this;

      self.cancel.on('click.raty', function(evt) {
        self.score.removeAttr('value');

        if (self.opt.click) {
          self.opt.click.call(self, null, evt);
        }
      });
    }, _bindOut: function() {
      var self = this;

      $(this).on('mouseleave.raty', function(evt) {
        var score = parseFloat(self.score.val()) || undefined;

        methods._apply.call(self, score);
        methods._target.call(self, score, evt);

        if (self.opt.mouseout) {
          self.opt.mouseout.call(self, score, evt);
        }
      });
    }, _bindOutCancel: function() {
      var self = this;

      self.cancel.on('mouseleave.raty', function(evt) {
        $(this).attr('src', self.opt.path + self.opt.cancelOff);

        if (self.opt.mouseout) {
          self.opt.mouseout.call(self, self.score.val() || null, evt);
        }
      });
    }, _bindOverCancel: function() {
      var self = this;

      self.cancel.on('mouseover.raty', function(evt) {
        $(this).attr('src', self.opt.path + self.opt.cancelOn);

        self.stars.attr('src', self.opt.path + self.opt.starOff);

        methods._target.call(self, null, evt);

        if (self.opt.mouseover) {
          self.opt.mouseover.call(self, null);
        }
      });
    }, _bindOver: function() {
      var self   = this,
          that   = $(self),
          action = self.opt.half ? 'mousemove.raty' : 'mouseover.raty';

      self.stars.on(action, function(evt) {
        var score = parseInt(this.alt, 10);

        if (self.opt.half) {
          var position = parseFloat((evt.pageX - $(this).offset().left) / self.opt.size),
              plus     = (position &gt; .5) ? 1 : .5;

          score = score - 1 + plus;

          methods._fill.call(self, score);

          if (self.opt.precision) {
            score = score - plus + position;
          }

          methods._roundStars.call(self, score);

          that.data('score', score);
        } else {
          methods._fill.call(self, score);
        }

        methods._target.call(self, score, evt);

        if (self.opt.mouseover) {
          self.opt.mouseover.call(self, score, evt);
        }
      });
    }, _callback: function(options) {
      for (i in options) {
        if (typeof this.opt[options[i]] === 'function') {
          this.opt[options[i]] = this.opt[options[i]].call(this);
        }
      }
    }, _createCancel: function() {
      var that   = $(this),
          icon   = this.opt.path + this.opt.cancelOff,
          cancel = $('&lt;img /&gt;', { src: icon, alt: 'x', title: this.opt.cancelHint, 'class': 'raty-cancel' });

      if (this.opt.cancelPlace == 'left') {
        that.prepend('&#160;').prepend(cancel);
      } else {
        that.append('&#160;').append(cancel);
      }

      return cancel;
    }, _createScore: function() {
      return $('&lt;input /&gt;', { type: 'hidden', name: this.opt.scoreName }).appendTo(this);
    }, _createStars: function() {
      var that = $(this);

      for (var i = 1; i &lt;= this.opt.number; i++) {
        var title = methods._getHint.call(this, i),
            icon  = (this.opt.score &amp;&amp; this.opt.score &gt;= i) ? 'starOn' : 'starOff';

        icon = this.opt.path + this.opt[icon];

        $('&lt;img /&gt;', { src : 'http://static-q.blogo.it/s/sf/img/blank.gif'/*icon*/, "alt": i, "title": title, "class": icon }).appendTo(this);

        if (this.opt.space) {
          that.append((i &lt; this.opt.number) ? '&#160;' : '');
        }
      }

      return that.children('img');
    }, _error: function(message) {
      $(this).html(message);

      $.error(message);
    }, _fill: function(score) {
      var self  = this,
          hash  = 0;

      for (var i = 1; i &lt;= self.stars.length; i++) {
        var star   = self.stars.eq(i - 1),
            select = self.opt.single ? (i == score) : (i &lt;= score);

        if (self.opt.iconRange &amp;&amp; self.opt.iconRange.length &gt; hash) {
          var irange = self.opt.iconRange[hash],
              on     = irange.on  || self.opt.starOn,
              off    = irange.off || self.opt.starOff,
              icon   = select ? on : off;

          if (i &lt;= irange.range) {
            star.attr('src', 'http://static-q.blogo.it/s/sf/img/blank.gif'/*self.opt.path + icon*/);
            star.attr('class', icon);
          }

          if (i == irange.range) {
            hash++;
          }
        } else {
          var icon = select ? 'starOn' : 'starOff';

          star.attr('src', 'http://static-q.blogo.it/s/sf/img/blank.gif'/*this.opt.path + this.opt[icon]*/);
          star.attr('class', icon);
        }
      }
    }, _getHint: function(score) {
      var hint = this.opt.hints[score - 1];
      return (hint === '') ? '' : (hint || score);
    }, _lock: function() {
      var score = parseInt(this.score.val(), 10), // TODO: 3.1 &gt;&gt; [['1'], ['2'], ['3', '.1', '.2']]
          hint  = score ? methods._getHint.call(this, score) : this.opt.noRatedMsg;

      $(this).data('readonly', true).css('cursor', '').attr('title', hint);

      this.score.attr('readonly', 'readonly');
      this.stars.attr('title', hint);

      if (this.cancel) {
        this.cancel.hide();
      }
    }, _roundStars: function(score) {
      var rest = (score - Math.floor(score)).toFixed(2);

      if (rest &gt; this.opt.round.down) {
        var icon = 'starOn';                                 // Up:   [x.76 .. x.99]

        if (this.opt.halfShow &amp;&amp; rest &lt; this.opt.round.up) { // Half: [x.26 .. x.75]
          icon = 'starHalf';
        } else if (rest &lt; this.opt.round.full) {             // Down: [x.00 .. x.5]
          icon = 'starOff';
        }

        this.stars.eq(Math.ceil(score) - 1).attr('src', 'http://static-q.blogo.it/s/sf/img/blank.gif'/*this.opt.path + this.opt[icon]*/);
        this.stars.eq(Math.ceil(score) - 1).attr('class', icon);
      }                              // Full down: [x.00 .. x.25]
    }, _target: function(score, evt) {
      if (this.opt.target) {
        var target = $(this.opt.target);

        if (target.length === 0) {
          methods._error.call(this, 'Target selector invalid or missing!');
        }

        if (this.opt.targetFormat.indexOf('{score}') &lt; 0) {
          methods._error.call(this, 'Template "{score}" missing!');
        }

        var mouseover = evt &amp;&amp; evt.type == 'mouseover';

        if (score === undefined) {
          score = this.opt.targetText;
        } else if (score === null) {
          score = mouseover ? this.opt.cancelHint : this.opt.targetText;
        } else {
          if (this.opt.targetType == 'hint') {
            score = methods._getHint.call(this, Math.ceil(score));
          } else if (this.opt.precision) {
            score = parseFloat(score).toFixed(1);
          }

          if (!mouseover &amp;&amp; !this.opt.targetKeep) {
            score = this.opt.targetText;
          }
        }

        if (score) {
          score = this.opt.targetFormat.toString().replace('{score}', score);
        }

        if (target.is(':input')) {
          target.val(score);
        } else {
          target.html(score);
        }
      }
    }, _unlock: function() {
      $(this).data('readonly', false).css('cursor', 'pointer').removeAttr('title');

      this.score.removeAttr('readonly', 'readonly');

      for (var i = 0; i &lt; this.opt.number; i++) {
        this.stars.eq(i).attr('title', methods._getHint.call(this, i + 1));
      }

      if (this.cancel) {
        this.cancel.css('display', '');
      }
    }, cancel: function(click) {
      return this.each(function() {
        if ($(this).data('readonly') !== true) {
          methods[click ? 'click' : 'score'].call(this, null);
          this.score.removeAttr('value');
        }
      });
    }, click: function(score) {
      return $(this).each(function() {
        if ($(this).data('readonly') !== true) {
          methods._apply.call(this, score);

          if (!this.opt.click) {
            methods._error.call(this, 'You must add the "click: function(score, evt) { }" callback.');
          }

          this.opt.click.call(this, score, { type: 'click' });

          methods._target.call(this, score);
        }
      });
    }, destroy: function() {
      return $(this).each(function() {
        var that = $(this),
            raw  = that.data('raw');

        if (raw) {
          that.off('.raty').empty().css({ cursor: raw.style.cursor, width: raw.style.width }).removeData('readonly');
        } else {
          that.data('raw', that.clone()[0]);
        }
      });
    }, getScore: function() {
      var score = [],
          value ;

      $(this).each(function() {
        value = this.score.val();

        score.push(value ? parseFloat(value) : undefined);
      });

      return (score.length &gt; 1) ? score : score[0];
    }, readOnly: function(readonly) {
      return this.each(function() {
        var that = $(this);

        if (that.data('readonly') !== readonly) {
          if (readonly) {
            that.off('.raty').children('img').off('.raty');

            methods._lock.call(this);
          } else {
            methods._binds.call(this);
            methods._unlock.call(this);
          }

          that.data('readonly', readonly);
        }
      });
    }, reload: function() {
      return methods.set.call(this, {});
    }, score: function() {
      return arguments.length ? methods.setScore.apply(this, arguments) : methods.getScore.call(this);
    }, set: function(settings) {
      return this.each(function() {
        var that   = $(this),
            actual = that.data('settings'),
            news   = $.extend({}, actual, settings);

        that.raty(news);
      });
    }, setScore: function(score) {
      return $(this).each(function() {
        if ($(this).data('readonly') !== true) {
          methods._apply.call(this, score);
          methods._target.call(this, score);
        }
      });
    }
  };

  $.fn.raty = function(method) {
    if (methods[method]) {
      return methods[method].apply(this, Array.prototype.slice.call(arguments, 1));
    } else if (typeof method === 'object' || !method) {
      return methods.init.apply(this, arguments);
    } else {
      $.error('Method ' + method + ' does not exist!');
    }
  };

  $.fn.raty.defaults = {
    cancel        : false,
    cancelHint    : 'Cancel this rating!',
    cancelOff     : 'cancel-off.png',
    cancelOn      : 'cancel-on.png',
    cancelPlace   : 'left',
    click         : undefined,
    half          : false,
    halfShow      : true,
    hints         : ['bad', 'poor', 'regular', 'good', 'gorgeous'],
    iconRange     : undefined,
    mouseout      : undefined,
    mouseover     : undefined,
    noRatedMsg    : 'Not rated yet!',
    number        : 5,
    numberMax     : 20,
    path          : '',
    precision     : false,
    readOnly      : false,
    round         : { down: .25, full: .6, up: .76 },
    score         : undefined,
    scoreName     : 'score',
    single        : false,
    size          : 16,
    space         : true,
    starHalf      : 'star-half.png',
    starOff       : 'star-off.png',
    starOn        : 'star-on.png',
    target        : undefined,
    targetFormat  : '{score}',
    targetKeep    : false,
    targetText    : '',
    targetType    : 'hint',
    width         : undefined
  };

})(jQuery);

var ratingManager = new RatingManager(window, $, BlogoUser, BlogoConfig);

ratingManager
.setUrl('http://www.cineblog.it/ajax/rate/submit')
.setRatingValue(3.89)
.setRatingCount(72)
.setPostId(34099)
.setCommunityUrl('http://community.cineblog.it/entra?returnUrl=')
.setMessages({"messageVoted":"Nessun voto. Potresti essere tu il primo!","messageAlreadyVoted":"Attenzione: il tuo voto &egrave; stato gi&agrave; registrato.","messageVoting":"Votazione in corso. Attendere prego...","messageLabelOn":"su","messageLabelBased":"basato","messageLabelVote":"voto","messageLabelVotes":"voti","messageRegistered":"Grazie, il tuo voto &egrave; stato registrato correttamente.","messageError":"Attenzione: si &egrave; verificato un errore durante la votazione.","messageAuthRequired":"Per votare devi prima autenticarti, tra pochi secondi sarai rediretto alla pagina di login."})
.init();

    //--&gt;
  </script>
 </body>
</html>
